(Introduction)
Oh heartache, oh burning soul
Oh lost love, oh pained hope
I had dreams and I had faith
But your face brought me pain

(Verse 1)
I used to dream we'd soar together in the sky
Building our world, racing against time
But your love was a trick, just a lie
It shattered my dreams, left me in pain's light

(Chorus)
Oh heartache, oh soul's cry
Why did you make me dream and build castles high?
Oh fake love, why did you waste me?

(Verse 2)
Oh Kanaan, oh disappointment of dreams
If only you understood, if only you knew
That you hardened me over the years
With you, dreams came to an end

(Bridge)
Oh deep wound, why won't you heal?
My pain in my heart cuts like a knife

(Verse 3)
I try to stand, to rebuild my soul
Facing the world, shouting at the top of my voice
I am strong, nothing can break me
I'll keep dreaming and find someone who understands me

(Chorus)
Oh heartache, oh soul's cry
Why did you make me dream and build castles high?
Oh fake love, why did you waste me?

(Outro)
Oh lost years, oh past illusions
Today, I live for myself and start anew
To hell with your company, I won't look back
For today I am stronger, and continue my path without fear
